0                                   1982      74.              
                                    1983      75.                Orvyl 5 control blocks needed for internal display  
                                    1984      76.                  commands only.                                    
                                    1985      77.              
                                    1986      78.              COPY  SLISTMAC
                                    1987             =*******************************************************************
                                    1988             =*                                                                 *
                                    1989             =* Macros for the serialized manipulation of single linked lists   *
                                    1990             =* in memory.  These lists are of the PUSH/POP (LIFO) variety.     *
                                    1991             =* Serialization is achieved using the CDS and CS instructions.    *
                                    1992             =*                                                                 *
                                    1993             =*******************************************************************
0                                   1995             =*******************************************************************
                                    1996             =*                                                                 *
                                    1997             =* Single linked list head fields                                  *
                                    1998             =*                                                                 *
                                    1999             =*******************************************************************
                                    2000             =         MACRO
                                    2001             =&LAB     SHEAD
                                    2002             =         AIF   ('&LAB' EQ '').ERR
                                    2003             =&LAB     DS   0D                   Single linked CDS list
                                    2004             =&LAB.FP  DS    A                   Forward pointer
                                    2005             =&LAB.SEQ DS    A                   CDS sequence number
                                    2006             =         MEXIT
                                    2007             =.ERR     MNOTE 8,'Label (list name) required'
                                    2008             =         MEND
0                                   2010             =*******************************************************************
                                    2011             =*                                                                 *
                                    2012             =* Push an item onto a single linked list                          *
                                    2013             =*                                                                 *
                                    2014             =*******************************************************************
                                    2015             =         MACRO
                                    2016             =&LABEL   SPUSH &HEAD=,&ITEM=
                                    2017             =         LCLC  &X
                                    2018             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    2019             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    2020             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    2021             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    2022             =         AIF   ('&ITEM' EQ '').ERR2
                                    2024             =         LM    R14,R15,&HEAD       Get fwd ptr and sequence number
                                    2025             =         LA    RVR,&ITEM           Point to new item
                                    2026             =         LOOP  BEGIN
                                    2027             =         LA    RS,1(R15)           Increment sequence
                                    2028             =         MVC   &ITEM.(L'&HEAD.FP),&HEAD.FP Set item fwd ptr
                                    2029             =         CDS   R14,RVR,&HEAD       Add item to list
                                    2030             =         UNTIL (Z),END
                                    2032             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2033             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    2034             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2035             =.ERR2    MNOTE 8,'Item is a required parameter'
                                    2036             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    2037             =         MEND  ,

0                                   2039             =*******************************************************************
                                    2040             =*                                                                 *
                                    2041             =* Pop an item from a single linked list. Addr returned in RVR     *
                                    2042             =* (zero if the list was empty).                                   *
                                    2043             =*                                                                 *
                                    2044             =*******************************************************************
                                    2045             =         MACRO
                                    2046             =&LABEL   SPOP  &HEAD=
                                    2047             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    2048             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    2049             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    2050             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    2052             =         LM    RVR,RS,&HEAD        Get fwd and sequence number
                                    2053             =         LOOP  BEGIN
                                    2054             =         IF    (RVR,Z),EXIT        None to get
                                    2055             =         LR    R14,RVR             Point to first item
                                    2056             =         L     R14,0(R14)          Get fwd pointer
                                    2057             =         LA    R15,1(RS)           Increment sequence
                                    2058             =         CDS   RVR,R14,&HEAD       Remove item from list
                                    2059             =         UNTIL (Z),END
                                    2061             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2062             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    2063             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    2064             =         MEND  ,
0                                   2066             =*******************************************************************
                                    2067             =*                                                                 *
                                    2068             =* Get an available item from list (ptr returned in RVR). Memory   *
                                    2069             =* will be obtained if the list is empty.                          *
                                    2070             =*                                                                 *
                                    2071             =*******************************************************************
                                    2072             =         MACRO
                                    2073             =&LABEL   SAVAIL &HEAD=,&LEN=,&LOC=GLOBHI,&FIX=,&PAGE=
                                    2074             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    2075             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    2076             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    2077             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    2078             =         AIF   ('&LEN' EQ '').ERR2
                                    2079             =         SPOP  HEAD=&HEAD          pop a free item
                                    2080             =         IF    (RVR,Z),BEGIN       empty list
                                    2081             =         VMGET &LEN,LOC=&LOC,FIX=&FIX,PAGE=&PAGE
                                    2082             =         IF    ('LTR RVR,RVR',ZERO),'ABORT NO_MEM_&HEAD'
                                    2083             =         END   ,
                                    2084             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2085             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    2086             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2087             =.ERR2    MNOTE 8,'Len is a required parameter'
                                    2088             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    2089             =         MEND  ,

                                    3214             =*
                                    3215             =*        CITH -- Cache Information Table
                                    3216             =*
                                    3217             =* Cache buffers are chained of a queue in one of 16 hash tables.
                                    3218             =* The hash table is determined by the last 4 bits of the hash key.
                                    3219             =* This helps prevent lock contention because there are 16 locks.
                                    3220             =* The number of queues per hash table is determined by the number
                                    3221             =* of blocks defined for the cache.
                                    3222             =*

                                    3283             =*******************************************************************
                                    3284             =*                                                                 *
                                    3285             =* These macros are used to update double linked memory lists.     *
                                    3286             =* Serialization is achieved using the PLO instruction. If a       *
                                    3287             =* memory block containing the list head needs to be locked anyway *
                                    3288             =* then the macros in LSTMAC would be better than these.           *
                                    3289             =* Conversely any existing use of LSTMAC macros might be           *
                                    3290             =* converted to this mechanism to avoid using locking.             *
                                    3291             =*                                                                 *
                                    3292             =*******************************************************************
0                                   3294             =*******************************************************************

                                    3300             =&LAB     QHEAD

                                    8468  4 1118.     * The reserve resource is used for two situations:
                                    8469  4 1119.     *
                                    8470  4 1120.     *  o During IO, it is obtained share for reads and exclusive
                                    8471  4 1121.     *    for writes. Since the system is obtaining the resource,
                                    8472  4 1122.     *    there will be no excessive delays and so not of interest
                                    8473  4 1123.     *    for this display.
                                    8474  4 1124.     *
                                    8475  4 1125.     *  o It is obtained exclusive for the RESERVE SVC. Here there
                                    8476  4 1126.     *    may be delays as the RELEASE is controled by a user program.
                                    8477  4 1127.     *
                                    8478  4 1128.     *  Therefore we will only display the reserve queue when it has
                                    8479  4 1129.     *  been obtained by the RESERVE SVC.
                                    8480  4 1130.     *
